MAIN DESCRIPTION_Dec2014=DIG! FIGHT! EXPLORE! BUILD! Join the community of millions of Terrarians!\n\nIn Terraria, every world is unique -- from the floating islands in the sky to the deepest level of The Underworld. Adventure to the ends of the earth, and battle villainous bosses along the way.  Defeat the Wall of Flesh to unlock Hardmode!  The world is your canvas and action-packed, sandbox adventures are just a pickaxe swing away!\n\nMULTIPLAYER - Local WiFi games support up to 4 players cross-platform on any mobile device!\n\n- 1250+ CRAFTING RECIPES - weapons, armor, potions, and more\n\n- 450+ ENEMIES!\n\n- 100+ BLOCK TYPES to build anything you can imagine!\n\n- 30+ PETS!\n\n- 20+ BOSSES!\n\n- Over a DOZEN environments to explore!\n\n- Dynamic water & lava, day/night cycles!\n\n- Create worlds as large as 4200 x 1200 tiles ("Small" worlds on PC)!\n\nEvery pixel of Terraria has been crafted for the BEST possible mobile experience -- including brand new touch controls and tutorials!\n\nFollow us on Twitter @Terraria_Logic and @505_Games\n\nLike us on Facebook at www.facebook.com/TerrariaOfficial and https://www.facebook.com/505Games\n\nVisit us on the web at www.terraria.org
2016_03_11_001=Dig! Fight! and Explore in a more expansive world over 2.5 times the size of what has been available thus far for Mobile Terrarians!  The Easter Bunny has left everyone a basket brimming with goodies - from needed fixes to the long-standing player request for more room to explore, this update is literally bursting at the seams with the inclusion of Expanded Worlds!
2016_03_11_002=That's right, you will now have the option of creating a more expansive world consisting of 4200 x 1200 tiles (equivalent to "Small" worlds on PC) OR a Normal World (1750 x 1000 tiles)!  Expanded worlds will also sort out some of the "interesting" worldgen quirks that existed on mobile to-date due to "overcrowding" of biomes.  Way cooler than a chocolate bunny or stale marshmallow chicks!

If you have an iPhone 4S or an iPad 2nd Gen, which both have less than 1GB of memory, you may experience performance issues if you create an Expanded World. **\n\nIn Terraria, every world is unique -- from the floating islands in the sky to the deepest level of The Underworld. Adventure to the ends of the earth, and battle villainous bosses along the way. 2016_04_06_002=This is the TRIAL version of Terraria for tablet and phone. \n \n**Requires Android OS 4.0.3 and above and 512MB RAM (1GB RAM recommended).**\n\n***If your device has less than 1GB of memory, you may experience performance issues if you create an Expanded World. The option to create Expanded Worlds is not available on devices with less than 512MB RAM.***
2016_04_06_003=Content update 1.02 adds exciting FROST MOON gameplay content, and doubles the number of save slots available to the player from three to six. A host of UI tweaks sees you gain 10 inventory slots; buffs can be cancelled on the Equip screen; stack speed is improved and we've made it harder to accidentally trash items.\n<br/><br/>\nFishing has been overhauled, and you'll be able to fish on the surface and other zones more effectively. Balancing issues are addressed, and the player and ores no longer glow so brightly - making the world more dangerous.\n<br/><br/>\nWe've addressed a number of stability issues, and solved the problem that led to game save times extending.\n<br/><br/>\nThis patch updates the game to version 1.0.2 - all players will need to be on the same version to engage in Local Play multiplayer together.
2016_05_26_001=*IMPORTANT* As well as Expanded Worlds, this update also includes a new Cloud save system which should ensure App stability returns. Providing you have Terraria installed on your device and have not deleted any local data, your existing Cloud save will work. All you need is a Google account with access to Google Drive. Chances are that if you use Gmail, YouTube, the Play Store, etc., you are already set up for this.\n\nThere are no additional steps needed to link this Google account to your Amazon device. The Google login is on the main menu and the rest is automatic.\n \nWe recommend you read this Forum post for full information regarding the new save system and contact us with any questions that you may have: http://forums.terraria.org/index.php?threads/terraria-mobile-amazon-update.42218/#post-946575

CONSOLETUTORIAL[19]=Switch to the Equip area by pressing R1.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[1]=Terraria is a game about adventuring to the ends of the World and defeating villainous bosses.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[20]=The Equip area is where you place armor and accessories.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[21]=Now switch to the Crafting area with L1 or R1.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[22]=Your gel and wood can be crafted into a torch. Select the torch recipe and press A to create it.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[23]=There are several categories of crafting items. You can switch between them with L2 and R2. For now, close the menu by pressing B.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[24]=To explore underground and craft better items, you'll need to dig and mine ore. Switch to your pickaxe.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[25]=Notice the vein of different ores. Mine them all by aiming with the Right Stick and holding R2.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[26]=As you dig deeper underground, you will find better ores. Some may require a better pickaxe to mine.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[27]=If you get stuck in a hole, you can place wood platforms to get out. Craft 5 wood platforms.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[28]=Switch to your wood platforms. (You may need to move them into your Inventory Bar item slots.)
CONSOLETUTORIAL[29]=Placing things is easier in the Manual Cursor Mode, which acts like a mouse. You can click the Right Stick to switch Cursor Modes. Aim and press R2 to place wood platforms. Build enough so you can jump out.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[2]=Use the Left Stick to move.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[30]=You can smelt the ore you mined into metal bars. To do this, stand near the furnace.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[31]=Craft as many metal bars as you can. (Make sure to switch to the 'tools & weapons' category in the Crafting menu.)
CONSOLETUTORIAL[32]=It's dangerous to be outside at night. You need to build a shelter.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[33]=Switch to the wood you collected from trees. (You may need to move them into your Inventory Bar item slots.)
CONSOLETUTORIAL[34]=Place wood to build walls and a ceiling at least 6 blocks high and 10 blocks wide. (If you need more wood, chop down trees.)
CONSOLETUTORIAL[35]=You'll need a door to get in and out. Remove 3 blocks from the bottom of a wall to make room. (Use the pickaxe to remove wood blocks.)
CONSOLETUTORIAL[36]=To craft a door, you need a work bench. Craft a work bench and place it inside your house. (If you need more wood, chop down trees.)
CONSOLETUTORIAL[37]=When you stand near a work bench or other crafting station (such as an anvil or furnace), more recipes will be available to craft.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[38]=Stand near your work bench and craft a door.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[39]=Now switch to the door and place it in the space in the wall. This can be tricky, and is easiest in the Manual Cursor Mode (click the Right Stick to switch).
CONSOLETUTORIAL[3]=Press A to jump.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[40]=You can open or close your door by standing next to it and pressing B or by walking through it.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[41]=If you want NPCs to move in, you'll need to furnish your house.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[42]=For NPCs, a room needs: a table (such as your work bench), a chair, and a light source (such as a torch).
CONSOLETUTORIAL[43]=Craft a chair at your work bench and place it in your house. (Make sure you also have a work bench or table in your house.)
CONSOLETUTORIAL[44]=Now place a torch on the walls or floor of your house.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[45]=You're almost done. To make your house safe, you'll need to panel its background with walls (such as wood walls).
CONSOLETUTORIAL[46]=Craft a bunch of wood walls at your work bench. (If you need more wood, chop down trees.)
CONSOLETUTORIAL[47]=Place the wood walls to panel the background of your house. This is easiest in the Auto Cursor Mode (click the Right Stick to switch). Make sure to cover the entire background.
CONSOLETUTORIAL[48]=This room is now livable. As you progress, new NPCs can move in if you have enough rooms for them.

MAIN DESCRIPTION_Expanded=Dig! Fight! and Explore a more expansive world over 2.5 times the size of what has been available thus far for Mobile Terrarians! This update is literally bursting at the seams with the inclusion of Expanded Worlds!\n\nThat's right, you will now have the option of creating a more expansive world consisting of 4200 x 1200 tiles (equivalent to "Small" worlds on PC) OR a Normal World (1750 x 1000 tiles)! Expanded Worlds will also sort out some of the "interesting" worldgen quirks that existed on mobile to-date due to "overcrowding" of biomes.  \n\nUnfortunately, one side effect of this update is that it will bring down the curtain on iOS 7 support.  Older devices that are not capable of iOS 8+ are just not capable of running what we have planned in a way that is acceptable. We remain fully committed to supporting iOS 8 and above from here on in.\n\nThis update also includes a second round of bug fixes from the ongoing list (thanks again for all of those informative bug reports - keep them coming!), with more to come!\n\nIMPORTANT NOTES:\n\niOS: If you have an iPhone 4S or an iPad 2nd Gen, which both have less than 1GB of memory, you may experience performance issues if you create an Expanded World.\n\nAndroid: If your device has less than 1GB of memory, you may experience performance issues if you create an Expanded World. The option to create Expanded Worlds is not available on devices with less than 512MB.

TUTORIAL[10]=Switch to your sword by touching the sword icon in the Inventory Bar.
TUTORIAL[11]=An evil monster has appeared. Defeat it with your sword by using the joystick on the right.
TUTORIAL[12]=Terraria is full of monsters, especially at night. Luckily you can find weapons, food, and potions to help you.
TUTORIAL[13]=Killing that slime gave you a gel. If you had wood to combine it with, you could craft a torch. Let's gather some wood.
TUTORIAL[14]=Move to the right to continue with the tutorial.
TUTORIAL[15]=To chop down a tree you must use an axe. Switch to your axe.
TUTORIAL[16]=Chop down a tree by touching a nearby trunk OR by using the joystick on the right.
TUTORIAL[17]=Items you pick up go into your Inventory. Touch the [...] slot to open the Inventory Menu.
TUTORIAL[18]=This is your Inventory. The top row of item slots is your Inventory Bar. You can rearrange items by dragging them around.
TUTORIAL[19]=Touch the tab with the head icon to switch to the Equip area.
TUTORIAL[1]=Terraria is a game about adventuring to the ends of the World and defeating villainous bosses. Touch here to get started.
TUTORIAL[20]=The Equip area is where you place armor and accessories.
TUTORIAL[21]=Touch the tab with the anvil/work bench icon to switch to the Crafting area.
TUTORIAL[22]=Your gel and wood can be crafted into a torch. Select the torch recipe and tap the CRAFT button.
TUTORIAL[23]=Close the menu.
TUTORIAL[24]=To explore underground and craft better items, you'll need to dig and mine ore. Switch to your pickaxe.
TUTORIAL[25]=Notice the vein of different ores. Mine them all by touching nearby ore blocks OR by using the joystick on the right.
TUTORIAL[26]=As you dig deeper underground, you will find better ores. Some may require a better pickaxe to mine.
TUTORIAL[27]=If you get stuck in a hole, you can place wood platforms to get out. Craft 5 wood platforms.
TUTORIAL[28]=Switch to your wood platforms. (You may need to move them into your Inventory Bar item slots.)
TUTORIAL[29]=Place the platforms by touching the screen where you want to put them. Build enough so you can jump out of the hole.
TUTORIAL[2]=Use the joystick on the left side of the screen to move.
TUTORIAL[30]=You can smelt the ore you mined into metal bars. To do this, stand near the furnace.
TUTORIAL[31]=Craft as many metal bars as you can. (Make sure to switch to the 'tools & weapons' category in the Crafting menu.)
TUTORIAL[32]=It's dangerous to be outside at night. You need to build a shelter.
TUTORIAL[33]=Switch to the wood you collected from trees. (You may need to move them into your Inventory Bar item slots.)
TUTORIAL[34]=Place wood to build walls and a ceiling at least 6 blocks high and 10 blocks wide. (If you need more wood, chop down trees.)
TUTORIAL[35]=You'll need a door to get in and out. Remove 3 blocks from the bottom of a wall to make room. (Use a pickaxe to remove wood blocks.)
TUTORIAL[36]=To craft a door, you need a work bench. Craft a work bench and place it inside your house. (If you need more wood, chop down trees.)
TUTORIAL[37]=When you stand near a work bench or other crafting station (such as an anvil or furnace), more recipes will be available to craft.
TUTORIAL[38]=Stand near your work bench and craft a door.
TUTORIAL[39]=Now place the door by switching to it and touching the top of the space in the wall.
TUTORIAL[3]=Slide the joystick up to jump.
TUTORIAL[40]=You can open or close your door by touching it or by walking through it.
TUTORIAL[41]=If you want NPCs to move in, you'll need to furnish your house.
TUTORIAL[42]=For NPCs, a room needs: a table (such as your work bench), a chair, and a light source (such as a torch).
TUTORIAL[43]=Craft a chair at your work bench and place it in your house. (Make sure you also have a work bench or table in your house.)
TUTORIAL[44]=Now place a torch on the walls or floor of your house.
TUTORIAL[45]=You're almost done. To make your house safe, you'll need to panel its background with walls (such as wood walls).
TUTORIAL[46]=Craft a bunch of wood walls at your work bench. (If you need more wood, chop down trees.)
TUTORIAL[47]=Place the wood walls to panel the background of your house. Make sure to cover the entire background.
TUTORIAL[48]=This room is now livable. As you progress, new NPCs can move in if you have enough rooms for them.
TUTORIAL[49]=The Guide is the first NPC who can move in. You can touch him for game hints or crafting info.
TUTORIAL[4]=You can fall through wood platforms by sliding the joystick down. Try falling through the platform.
TUTORIAL[50]=If you ever want to destroy furniture or background walls, you can craft a hammer to do so.
TUTORIAL[51]=That's it! This floating island is pretty small, but there's some cool stuff hidden around.
TUTORIAL[52]=When you're ready, exit the tutorial and create yourself a whole new World!
TUTORIAL[5]=Now jump out by sliding the joystick up.
TUTORIAL[6]=Touch the screen near your character to perform actions with your current item.
TUTORIAL[7]=Tools and weapons can also be controlled with the joystick on the right side of the screen.
TUTORIAL[8]=Slide the joystick on the right to mine, chop, or attack in that direction.
TUTORIAL[9]=At the top of your screen is the Inventory Bar. You can switch between items by touching their icons.

TUTORIAL_3DS_01=Welcome to Terraria, a world of adventure with infinite possibilities. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_02=You're going to see incredible things and fight terrifying enemies, but first you need to learn the basics. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_03=Use <<CIRCLEPAD>> to move around. Go on, have a little run about.
TUTORIAL_3DS_03_TIP=Move with <<CIRCLEPAD>>
TUTORIAL_3DS_04=Press <<B>> to jump. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_04_TIP=Jump with <<B>>
TUTORIAL_3DS_05=You can fall through wood platforms by pressing <<CIRCLEPAD>> downwards. Try falling through the platform.
TUTORIAL_3DS_05_TIP=Fall through the platform using <<CIRCLEPAD>>
TUTORIAL_3DS_06=Now jump out by pressing <<B>>. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_06_TIP=Press <<B>> to jump out
TUTORIAL_3DS_07=To perform actions with your current item, press (or hold) <<Y>>.
TUTORIAL_3DS_07_TIP=Press <<Y>> to perform actions and use items
TUTORIAL_3DS_08=The Inventory Bar holds the first 10 items in your Inventory. You can switch between items by touching them, or with <<L>> and <<R>>.
TUTORIAL_3DS_09=Now switch to your sword.
TUTORIAL_3DS_09_TIP=Select your sword
TUTORIAL_3DS_10=It's time to kill something! Defeat the Green Slime with your sword by pressing <<Y>>!
TUTORIAL_3DS_10_TIP=Kill the green slime
TUTORIAL_3DS_11=Terraria is full of monsters, especially at night. Luckily, there are weapons you can find to fight them off. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_12=If you get hurt, you'll heal over time, or you can use food or healing potions.
TUTORIAL_3DS_13=Killing that slime gave you a gel. This is half of what you need to craft a torch! 
TUTORIAL_3DS_14=You also need wood, so let's find some.
TUTORIAL_3DS_15=To get wood, you need to chop down trees. Switch to your axe, and press and hold <<Y>> to use it.
TUTORIAL_3DS_15_TIP=Chop down a tree with <<Y>>
TUTORIAL_3DS_16=All the items you pick up go into the Inventory. Tap <<BACKPACK>> on the Touch Screen to open the Inventory menu.
TUTORIAL_3DS_16_TIP=Tap <<BACKPACK>> to open the Inventory Menu
TUTORIAL_3DS_17=The Inventory menu is split into sections, which are spread across tabs at the top of your Touch Screen. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_18=You are now in your main Inventory. The top two rows are the items that will appear in your Inventory Bar.
TUTORIAL_3DS_19=You can touch the slots to move and drop stacks of items, or use <<CONTROLPAD>> and <<A>> to select and drop them. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_20=Switch to the Equip menu by tapping the tab with the head icon, or by pressing <<L>> or <<R>>.
TUTORIAL_3DS_20_TIP=Switch to the Equip menu
TUTORIAL_3DS_21=The Equip menu is where you place armor and accessories.
TUTORIAL_3DS_22=Items in Vanity slots appear on your character, but do not give armor bonuses. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_23=You can also find information on your status effects here.
TUTORIAL_3DS_24=Switch to the Crafting menu by tapping the anvil/workbench tab, or by pressing <<L>> or <<R>>.
TUTORIAL_3DS_24_TIP=Switch to the Crafting menu
TUTORIAL_3DS_25=Craftable recipes appear here. Tap to select the torch recipe, or use <<CONTROLPAD>> and <<A>>. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_26=The recipe information on the top screen tells you about all the ingredients you need. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_27=The columns on the left are various Crafting categories. You can switch between them by tapping on them, or use <<Y>>.
TUTORIAL_3DS_28=Remember the slime you just killed? The gel and wood you gathered can be crafted into a torch.
TUTORIAL_3DS_29=Tap on the Craft button or press <<A>> to craft the recipe and create a torch!
TUTORIAL_3DS_29_TIP=Craft a torch
TUTORIAL_3DS_30=Now close the Inventory menu by pressing <<B>>.
TUTORIAL_3DS_30_TIP=Close the Inventory menu
TUTORIAL_3DS_31=To create better items and explore the vast underground, you will need to dig down and mine ore with a pickaxe. Switch to your pickaxe.
TUTORIAL_3DS_31_TIP=Select your pickaxe
TUTORIAL_3DS_32=Nearby there is a vein of copper ore. Mine it all. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_32_TIP=Mine all ores
TUTORIAL_3DS_33=For more precision in your mining, you can switch to Building Mode by pressing <<BUILDMODE>> on your Touch Screen.
TUTORIAL_3DS_33_TIP=Switch to Building Mode
TUTORIAL_3DS_34=As you dig deeper underground, you will find better ores. Some may require a better pickaxe to mine.
TUTORIAL_3DS_35=If you get stuck in a hole, you can place wood platforms to get out.
TUTORIAL_3DS_36=Craft 5 wood platforms, and build enough platforms to jump out of there.
TUTORIAL_3DS_36_TIP=Build platforms to climb out
TUTORIAL_3DS_37=You can build and mine directly using the Touch Screen or <<CONTROLPAD>>. Moving <<CIRCLEPAD>> partially in any direction, will build or mine blocks in your direct vicinity.
TUTORIAL_3DS_38=In combat, auto-aim will identify targets. You can lock to a target by pressing <<X>>.
TUTORIAL_3DS_39=Now that you have found some ore, you can smelt it into metal bars. Find the furnace, and stand next to it.
TUTORIAL_3DS_39_TIP=Stand near the furnace
TUTORIAL_3DS_40=Craft as many metal bars as you can. Make sure to switch to the 'tools and weapons' category in the Crafting menu.
TUTORIAL_3DS_40_TIP=Craft as many metal bars as you can
TUTORIAL_3DS_41=Worlds in Terraria are just like your own: it turns day and night.
TUTORIAL_3DS_42=It's dangerous to be outside at night. Better build a shelter before it gets dark.
TUTORIAL_3DS_43=To start, build walls and a ceiling. Give yourself plenty of room inside. If you don't have enough wood (or stone), gather more.
TUTORIAL_3DS_44=A shelter must be at least 6 blocks high and 10 blocks wide.
TUTORIAL_3DS_44_TIP=Build a shelter of 6 by 10 blocks
TUTORIAL_3DS_45=You'll need a door to get in and out. Remove 3 blocks from the bottom of a wall to make room.
TUTORIAL_3DS_46=Use a pickaxe to remove wood blocks or stone blocks.
TUTORIAL_3DS_47=To craft a door, you need a workbench. Craft a workbench and place it inside your house.
TUTORIAL_3DS_47_TIP=Craft and place a workbench
TUTORIAL_3DS_48=When you are standing near a workbench or other crafting station (such as an anvil or furnace), the Crafting menu will show more recipes that are available.
TUTORIAL_3DS_49=Stand near your workbench and craft a door.
TUTORIAL_3DS_49_TIP=Craft a door
TUTORIAL_3DS_50=Now place the door by selecting it and  tapping in the space in the wall. Use Building Mode for greater precision.
TUTORIAL_3DS_50_TIP=Place a door
TUTORIAL_3DS_51=You're almost done! To make your house safe, you will need to panel the background of your house with walls (such as wood walls).
TUTORIAL_3DS_52=Craft some wood walls and panel the background of your house. Use Building Mode if you need to. 
TUTORIAL_3DS_53=Make sure to cover the background well.
TUTORIAL_3DS_53_TIP=Panel the background of the house
TUTORIAL_3DS_54=Your house is now safe. You can even get NPCs to move in! 
TUTORIAL_3DS_55=For a room to be livable for NPCs, it needs a table (such as your work bench), a chair, and a light source (such as a torch).
TUTORIAL_3DS_56=Let's try and see if you can get someone to move in. Craft a chair and place it in your house.
TUTORIAL_3DS_56_TIP=Craft and place a chair
TUTORIAL_3DS_57=Now place a torch on the walls or floor of your house. Use Building Mode if you need to.
TUTORIAL_3DS_57_TIP=Place a torch in your house
TUTORIAL_3DS_58=This room is now livable for NPCs. As you progress, there are many NPCs who can move into your house if you have enough livable rooms for them.
TUTORIAL_3DS_59=The Guide is the first NPC who can move into your house. You can talk to him for tips or details about crafting ingredients.
TUTORIAL_3DS_60=If you ever want to destroy any furniture or background walls, you can craft a hammer to do so.
TUTORIAL_3DS_61=So there you have it: you have learned the basics of Terraria! Exploring, building, fighting and crafting: you can do it all.
TUTORIAL_3DS_62=There are only a few areas to explore on this floating island. When you are ready, exit the tutorial and create yourself a whole new World!
TUTORIAL_3DS_63=Press <<A>> to continue
TUTORIAL_3DS_64_TIP=Exit the tutorial and create your own world!
